  <script>

    // Ensure loading dialog is closed when coming back with back button

    window.addEventListener('pageshow', function (event) {

        if (event.persisted) {

            // Page restored from bfcache

            Swal.close();

        } else {

            // In case it's not persisted but modal still exists

            Swal.close();

        }

    });



    function loadScriptWithFallback(cdnUrl, localUrl, isHead = false) {

        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {

            const script = document.createElement('script');

            script.src = cdnUrl;

            script.onload = () => {

                //console.log(`${cdnUrl} loaded`);

                resolve();

            };

            script.onerror = () => {

                console.warn(`${cdnUrl} failed. Loading fallback: ${fallbackUrl}`);

                const fallbackScript = document.createElement('script');

                fallbackScript.src = fallbackUrl;

                fallbackScript.onload = resolve;

                fallbackScript.onerror = reject;

                document.body.appendChild(fallbackScript);

            };

            if (isHead) {

                document.head.appendChild(script);

            }

            else {

                document.body.appendChild(script);

            }

        });

    }

</script> <!-- JQuery min js -->

    // Force browsers to reload the page when navigating back:

    window.addEventListener("pageshow", function (event) {

        if (event.persisted || (window.performance && window.performance.navigation.type === 2)) {

            window.location.reload();

        }

    });

  <script>

    let currentPage = 1;

    const loadMoreBtn = document.getElementById('load-more-btn');

    const notifContainer = document.getElementById('notification-content');



    loadMoreBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {

        currentPage++;

        loadMoreBtn.disabled = true;

        loadMoreBtn.innerText = 'Memuat...';



        fetch(`/ajax/notification?page=${currentPage}`)

            .then(res => res.json())

            .then(data => {

                data.notifications.forEach(notif => {

                    notifContainer.innerHTML += `

                        <a class="d-flex p-3 border-bottom notification-item"

                            style="background: ${notif.status == 0 ? '#f6f6fb' : '#fff'}"

                            href="#" data-notification-id="${notif.id}">

                            <div class="ms-3">

                                <h5 class="notification-label mb-1">${notif.message}</h5>

                                <div class="notification-subtext">${notif.created_at}</div>

                            </div>

                            <div class="ms-auto">

                                <i class="las la-angle-right text-end text-muted"></i>

                            </div>

                        </a>

                    `;

                });



                if (currentPage >= data.last_page) {

                    loadMoreBtn.remove();

                } else {

                    loadMoreBtn.disabled = false;

                    loadMoreBtn.innerText = 'Muat lebih banyak';

                }

            });

    });

</script> 

  <script>

    $(document).ready(function() {

        setDataTableDefaultConfig();

        //untuk menutup alert secara otomatis

        $(".alert").hide();

        $(".alert").fadeTo(5000, 500).slideUp(100, function() {

            $(".alert").slideUp(500);

        });

        $("table").on('draw.dt', function() {

            $('.dataTables_empty').html('Tidak ditemukan data yang cocok');

            $('.dataTables_processing').html('Memproses.....');

            $("td").has("button:not(.no-action),a:not(.no-action)").addClass("d-flex")

        });

    });



    function setDataTableDefaultConfig() {

        try {

            $.extend(true, $.fn.dataTable.defaults, {

                stateSave: true

            });

        } catch (error) {

            console.log('error datatable default config');

        }

    }

</script> 

  <script>

    //handle dropdown close if click outside

    $(document).ready(function() {

        $(document).on('click', function(event) {

            if (!$(event.target).closest('.dropdown > * ').length) {

                $('.dropdown').removeClass('show');

            }

        });

    });



    $('input[type="file"]').each(function() {

        $(this).change(function(e) {

            const fileInput = e.target;

            var fileName = '';

            if (fileInput.files.length > 0) {

                fileName = fileInput.files[0].name;

            }

            $(fileInput).parent().css("--content", '"' + fileName + '"')

        });

    })



    $('input[type="file"]:not(.d-none)').each(function() {

        $(this).wrap(`<label class='file-input-wrapper d-block border'></label>`);

    });

</script> 

  <script>

    function markAllRead() {

        var btnRead = $('#btn-mark-all-read');

        showLoadingDialog();

        $.ajax({

            url: "https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/notification-mark-all-read",

            method: 'GET',

            success: function (response) {

                if (response.success) {

                    var totalUnreadText = btnRead.parent().parent().find('.total-unread-text')

                    if (totalUnreadText) {

                        totalUnreadText.html('Anda tidak punya notifikasi yang belum dibaca')

                    }

                    var notificationItems = $('#notification-content').find('.notification-item')

                    if (notificationItems) {

                        notificationItems.each(function (i) {

                            $(this).removeAttr('style')

                            $(this).css('background-color', '#fff')

                        })

                    }

                    setTimeout(() => {

                        btnRead.addClass('d-none');

                        Swal.close();



                        // Remove green circle

                        if (!($('.notification-icon').find('.pulse').hasClass('d-none'))) {

                            $('.notification-icon').find('.pulse').addClass('d-none');

                        }

                    }, 2000);

                }

            },

            error: function (e) {

                showErrorDialog('Terjadi kesalahan');

                Swal.close();

                console.log(e)

            }

        });

    }

    $(document).ready(function() {

        $('#btn-mark-all-read').on('click', function () {

            markAllRead();

        })



        $(document).on('click', '.notification-item', function(e) {

            e.preventDefault();



            var notificationId = $(this).data('notification-id');



            if (notificationId) {

                $.ajax({

                    url: "https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/notification/" + notificationId,

                    method: 'GET',

                    success: function(response) {

                        if (response.success) {

                            var notificationType = response.data.type;

                            var redirectUrl = '';



                            if (notificationType === 'Task Notif') {

                                redirectUrl =

                                    `/task-approval/${response.data.task_id}`;

                            } else if (notificationType == 'Task') {

                                redirectUrl =

                                    `/task/${response.data.data_id}`;

                            } else if (notificationType == 'Periode') {

                                redirectUrl =

                                    `/periode`;

                            } else if (notificationType == 'Terms') {

                                redirectUrl =

                                    `/term`;

                            } else if (notificationType == 'Status_Jobsite') {

                                redirectUrl =

                                    `/masterstatus`;

                            } else if (notificationType == 'Issue') {

                                redirectUrl =

                                    `/issue/${response.data.data_id}`;

                            } else if (notificationType == 'Communication') {

                                redirectUrl =

                                    `/communication/${response.data.data_id}`;

                            }

                            if (redirectUrl) {

                                window.location.href = redirectUrl;

                            }

                        } else {

                            alert('Failed to update notification status.');

                        }

                    },

                    error: function() {

                        alert('An error occurred.');

                    }

                });

            }

        });

    });





    $('input[type="file"]').each(function() {

        $(this).change(function(e) {

            const fileInput = e.target;

            var fileName = '';

            if (fileInput.files.length > 0) {

                fileName = fileInput.files[0].name;

            }

            $(fileInput).parent().css("--content", '"' + fileName + '"')

        });

    })



    $('input[type="file"]:not(.d-none)').each(function() {

        $(this).wrap(`<label class='file-input-wrapper d-block border'></label>`);

    });

            var cleaned = $(this).val().replace(/<[^>]+>/g, ''); // Menghapus semua tag HTML

            var output = cleaned.replace(/=[^=+\-/*^()A-Za-z0-9. ]+/g, '');

            $(this).parent().parent().removeClass("bg-white");

    function capitalize(s)

    {

        if (isNumber(s)) return s;

        return s && String(s[0]).toUpperCase() + String(s).slice(1);

    }



    function ucwords(str) {

        if (isNumber(str)) return str;

        return str ? str.replace(/\b\w/g, char => char.toUpperCase()) : str;

    }



    function isNumber(n) {

        return /^-?[\d.]+(?:e-?\d+)?$/.test(n);

    }



    const locale = 'id-ID'; // Indonesian



    function parseIndonesianDate(dateStr) {

        const bulan = {

            'Januari': '01',

            'Februari': '02',

            'Maret': '03',

            'April': '04',

            'Mei': '05',

            'Juni': '06',

            'Juli': '07',

            'Agustus': '08',

            'September': '09',

            'Oktober': '10',

            'November': '11',

            'Desember': '12'

        };



        const parts = dateStr.split(' '); // ['22', 'Mei', '2025', '08:44']

        if (parts.length < 4) return null;



        const day = parts[0].padStart(2, '0');

        const month = bulan[parts[1]];

        const year = parts[2];

        const time = parts[3];



        if (!month) return null;



        return new Date(`${year}-${month}-${day}T${time}`);

    }



    function formatDate(data, indonesianFormat = true) {

        const date = indonesianFormat ? parseIndonesianDate(data) : new Date(data);

        const options = {

            day: '2-digit',

            month: 'long', // show full Indonesian month (e.g., "Mei")

            year: 'numeric',

            hour: '2-digit',

            minute: '2-digit',

            hour12: false

        };

        const formatted = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, options).format(date);

        return `${formatted} WIB`;

    }



    function formatSimpleDate(data, indonesianFormat = true) {

        const date = indonesianFormat ? parseIndonesianDate(data) : new Date(data);

        if (!date) return '-';

        return new Intl.DateTimeFormat('id-ID', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' }).format(date);

    }



    function formatHourDate(data, indonesianFormat = true) {

        const date = indonesianFormat ? parseIndonesianDate(data) : new Date(data);

        if (!date) return '-';

        return new Intl.DateTimeFormat('id-ID', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', hour12: false }).format(date);

    }



    function isValidDate(d) {

        return !isNaN(new Date(d).getTime());

    }



    function getNumberOnly(str) {

        return str.replace(/\D/g, "");

    }



    $(document).on('submit', 'form', function () {

        showLoadingDialog();

    });



    function showLoadingDialog(message = 'Silahkan tunggu...') {

        Swal.fire({

            title: 'Loading...',

            icon: 'info',

            text: message,

            allowOutsideClick: false,

            backdrop: `

                rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4) !important;

                z-index: 99999 !important;

            `,

            customClass: {

                popup: 'custom-swal-popup'

            },

            didOpen: () => {

                Swal.showLoading();

                document.querySelector('.swal2-container').style.zIndex = '99999';

            },

            didClose: () => {

                Swal.hideLoading();

            }

        });

    }



    function showSuccessDialog(message = 'Berhasil') {

        Swal.fire({

            title: 'Berhasil',

            icon: 'success',

            text: message,

            timer: 2000,

            showConfirmButton: false,

            didOpen: () => {

                Swal.hideLoading();

            },

        });

    }



    function showWarningDialog(message = 'Peringatan') {

        Swal.fire({

            title: 'Peringatan',

            icon: 'warning',

            text: message,

            timer: 2000,

            showConfirmButton: false,

            didOpen: () => {

                Swal.hideLoading();

            },

        });

    }



    function showInfoDialog(message = 'Informasi') {

        Swal.fire({

            title: 'Informasi',

            icon: 'info',

            text: message,

            timer: 2000,

            showConfirmButton: false,

            didOpen: () => {

                Swal.hideLoading();

            },

        });

    }



    function showErrorDialog(message = 'Kesalahan terjadi pada sistem') {

        Swal.fire({

            title: 'Terjadi Kesalahan',

            icon: 'error',

            text: message,

            didOpen: () => {

                Swal.hideLoading();

            },

        });

    }



    function scrollTo(scrollTo) {

        if (scrollTo) {

            if (scrollTo.includes('#')) {

                scrollTo = scrollTo.split('#')[1];

            }

            const targetElement = document.getElementById(scrollTo);

            if (targetElement) {

                targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });

            }

        }

    }



    function getColor(index) {

        const colors = [

            "#1E44C5",

            "#B0005A",

            "#6100C4",

            "#59637A",

            "#569900",

            "#CC452A",

            "#269844",

            "#265ECF",

            "#C826B6",

            "#CCA12A",

            "#CC0060",

            "#0060CC",

            "#60CC00",

            "#CC6600",

            "#6000CC",

            "#00CC60",

            "#CC0030",

            "#CC9500",

            "#9500CC",

            "#0095CC"

        ];

        return colors[index];

    }

        function updateSiteTensionChart(data) {

            const period = $('#f_period').val();

            // Prepare full objects for Highcharts with level info

            const chartData = data.map(item => ({

                y: item.percentage,

                level: ucwords(item.level),

                status: item.status,

                changed: item.changed,

                communication_id: item.communication_id,

                communication_deleted: item.communication_deleted,

                date: period === '' ? formatHourDate(item.date, false) + ' WIB' : item.date,

                data: period === '' ? [] : item.data

            }));



            const dates = data.map(item => (period === '' ? formatSimpleDate(item.date, false) : item.date));

            const percentages = data.map(item => item.percentage);

            Highcharts.chart('site-tension-trend-container', {

                chart: {

                    type: 'line',

                    height: '40%',

                    spacingTop: 20

                },

                exporting: {

                    buttons: {

                        contextButton: {

                            y: -20

                        }

                    }

                },

                title: {

                    text: '',

                    align: 'left',

                    style: titleChartStyle

                },

                credits: {

                    enabled: false

                },

                xAxis: {

                    categories: dates,

                    title: {

                        text: 'Date',

                        enabled: false

                    }

                },

                yAxis: {

                    min: 0,

                    max: 100,

                    title: { text: 'Tension (%)' }

                },

                tooltip: {

                    useHTML: true,

                    shared: true,

                    outside: true,

                    followPointer: false,

                    stickOnContact: true,

                    formatter: function () {

                        const level = this.point.level || 'N/A';

                        let icon = this.point.status == 'up'

                            ? '<i class="fas fa-arrow-up text-danger"></i>'

                            : '<i class="fas fa-arrow-down text-success"></i>';

                        const date = this.point.date || this.x;

                        const data = this.point.data ?? [];

                        const url = "https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/communication";

                        const comId = this.point.communication_id;

                        let communicationList = data.length

                        ? '<ul class="ps-4">' + data.map((item, i) => {

                            const id = item.communication_id; // Ensure ID exists

                            const deleted = item.communication_deleted;

                            const title = `${ucwords(item.level)} (${item.percentage}%) - ${item.date} WIB`;

                            const button = deleted

                            ? `<a href="#" class='btn-communication-deleted'>${title}</a>`

                            : `<a href="${url}/${id}" target="_blank" class="title-communication-item">${title}</a>`;

                            return `<li>${button}</li>`;

                        }).join('') + '</ul>'

                        : (this.point.communication_deleted

                            ? `<a href="#" class='btn-communication-deleted'>Detail</a>`

                            : `<a href="${url}/${comId}" target="_blank" class="title-communication-item">Detail</a>`);

                        if (data.length > 0) {

                            return `

                                ${date}<br>

                                ${communicationList}

                            `;

                        }

                        return `

                            <b>${icon} ${level} - ${this.y}%</b><br>

                            ${date} - ${communicationList}

                        `;

                    }

                },

                series: [{

                    name: 'Site Tension',

                    data: chartData,

                    dataLabels: {

                        format: '{y} %',

                        style: {

                            fontSize: '16px'

                        }

                    }

                }],

                legend: {

                    enabled: false,

                },

                responsive: {

                    rules: [

                        {

                            condition: {

                                maxWidth: 500

                            },

                            chartOptions: {

                                chart: {

                                    height: '60%'

                                },

        function trendFilterOnChange() {

            $('.graph-skeleton').toggleClass('d-none');

            $('.trend-highcharts-figure').toggleClass('d-none');

            const period = $(this).val();

            $.ajax({

                url: "https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/dashboard",

                method: 'get',

                data: {

                    type: 'site-tension',

                    period: period

                },

                success: function (response) {

                    if (response.siteTension != null) {

                        updateSiteTensionChart(response.siteTension);

                    }

                },

                error: function (e) {

                    console.log(e)

                }

            });

        }



        function reportOnSubmit(e) {

            e.preventDefault();

            const dateStart = $('#date_start').val();

            const dateEnd = $('#date_end').val();

            const validated = datePickerValidation(dateStart, dateEnd);

            const isExecutive = $(this).data('is-executive');

            if (validated) {

                $('#report-modal').modal('hide');

                showLoadingDialog("Sedang mengumpulkan data untuk generate report...");

                if (isExecutive) {

                    window.location = "https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/report/executive?date_start=&date_end=";

                }

                else{

                    window.location = "https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/report?date_start="+dateStart+"&date_end="+dateEnd;

                }

            }

        }



        function datePickerValidation(dateStart, dateEnd) {

            if (dateStart === '') {

                $('.date-start-error').html('Harap pilih tanggal awal');

            }

            else {

                $('.date-start-error').html('');

            }

            if (dateEnd === '') {

                $('.date-end-error').html('Harap pilih tanggal akhir');

            }

            else {

                $('.date-end-error').html('');

            }



            return dateStart !== '' && dateEnd !== '';

        }

  <script>

        $(document).ready(function() {

            var $periodeSelect = $('#periodeSelect');

            var data = {"id":64,"jobsite_id":14,"nama_periode":"KIW1","tanggal_mulai":"2025-09-26","tanggal_selesai":"2025-12-31","status":"Aktif","isLock":"lock","is_started":1,"created_at":"2025-09-26T06:56:19.000000Z","updated_at":"2025-10-17T08:01:49.000000Z"};

            const selectedPeriodeYear = "2025";



            if (selectedPeriodeYear) {

                getListPeriode(selectedPeriodeYear, true);

            }



            if (data) {

                $periodeSelect.empty();

                var option = $('<option>', {

                    value: data.id,

                    text: data.nama_periode,

                    selected: true

                });



                $periodeSelect.append(option);

            }



            function getListPeriode(year, firstLoad=false) {

                if (year) {

                    $.ajax({

                        url: `/dashboard/periode`,

                        type: 'GET',

                        data: {

                            year: year,

                            jobsite: "14",

                        },

                        success: function(response) {

                            $periodeSelect.empty();

                            $periodeSelect.append('<option value="">Pilih Periode</option>');



                            $.each(response.data, function(index, period) {

                                var selected = '';

                                if (firstLoad && data.id == period.id) {

                                    selected = 'selected';

                                }

                                var option = `<option value="${period.id}" ${selected}>${period.nama_periode}</option>`;



                                $periodeSelect.append(option);

                            });

                        },

                        error: function(xhr) {

                            console.error('Gagal memuat data periode:', xhr.responseText);

                        }

                    });

                } else {

                    $periodeSelect.empty().append('<option value="">Pilih Periode</option>');

                }

            }



            var selectedYear = null;

            $('#year').change(function() {

                var selectedYear = $(this).val();



                getListPeriode(selectedYear)

            });



            if (selectedYear) {

                $('#year').val(selectedYear).trigger('change');

            }

        });

    </script>

  <script>

        const showData = (dataList, panelClass, urlPrefix, location = null) => {

            $(`.panel.${panelClass}`).show();

            $(`.panel.${panelClass} .row`).empty();



            dataList.forEach(data => {

                const parts = data.keterangan.split("|");

                if (panelClass === 'stakeholder') {

                    if (location !== null) {

                        parts.splice(1, 0, location);

                    }

                }

                const keterangan = parts.join(" | ");



                const url = `/${urlPrefix}/${data.id}`;

                let html, name;

                if (panelClass === 'isu') {

                    name = data.title;

                }

                else {

                    name = data.name;

                }

                if (data.id != 0) {

                    html = `<div class="col-12">

                        <a href="${url}" class="text-black"><div class="d-flex align-items-center">

                            <div class=" ms-2">

                                <h6 class="mb-0 ">${name}</h6>

                                <small class="mb-0">${keterangan}</small>

                            </div>

                            <div class="ms-auto">

                            <i class="fa fa-chevron-right"></i>

                            </div>

                        </div></a>

                        <hr class="m-1" style="background-color:#808590">

                    </div>`;

                }

                else {

                    html = `<div class="col-12 ">

                      <div class="d-flex align-items-center">

                            <div class=" ms-2">

                                <h6 class="mb-0 ">${name}</h6>

                            </div>

                        </div>

                    </div>`;

                }

                $(`.panel.${panelClass} .row`).append(html);

            });

        };

        function initMap() {

            map = L.map('map', {

                zoomControl: false

            })

            L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {

                attribution: '© <a href="https://www.openstreetmap.org/copyright">OpenStreetMap</a> contributors',

                // noWrap: true

            }).addTo(map);

            map.options.minZoom = 3;

        }

        initMap();



        const mode = {

            1: "PERUSAHAAN",

            0: "JOBSITE"

        };

        let currentMode = mode[0],

            zoom = 10;



        $("[name='map-option']").change(setMode)

        let layers = [];



        function setMode() {

            const val = $(this).val();

            if (val == 0) {

                currentMode = mode[0]

                zoom = 10;

                $(".marker-info").show()



            } else {

                $(".marker-info").hide()

                currentMode = mode[1]

                zoom = 7;

            }



            $(".panel.isu").hide()

            $(".panel.stakeholder").hide()

            generateMarker();

        }



        function generateMarkerInfo(data) {

            let html = "";

            for (const index in data) {

                const label = data[index].parent.replaceAll(' ', '').toLowerCase();

                const color = markerRingColor[data[index]["color"]];

                const iconUrl = `https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/markers/img/marker-${label}.png`;



                html += `<div class="d-flex col-md-4 align-items-center gap-2 col-auto p-2 px-4">

                    <img class="ht-40" src='${iconUrl}'/>

                    <div class="">

                        <p class="mb-0 fw-bold"> ${data[index]['parent']}</p>

                        <p class="mb-0">${data[index]["child"]}</p>

                    </div>

                </div>`;

            }



            $(".marker-info .row").empty().append(html)

        }

        generateMarkerInfo(dataInfoMarker)

            map.on('zoomend', function() {

                $(".panel.isu").hide()

                if (map.getZoom() < currZoom && mode[1] == currentMode) {

        const mstSiteTensionLevel = [

            25,

            50,

            75,

            100

        ];

        const mstSiteTensionColors = [

            'green',

            'yellow',

            'orange',

            'red'

        ];

        function generateJobsite(data, bounds) {

            let colorIndex = 0;

            if (data.siteTension) {

                colorIndex = mstSiteTensionLevel.findIndex(level => data.siteTension.percentage <= level);

            }

            //const color = markerColor[data.color || "#36AE7C"];

            const color = mstSiteTensionColors[colorIndex];

            const iconUrl = `https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/markers/img/marker-level-${color}.png`;

            var customIcon = L.icon({

                iconUrl: iconUrl,

                iconSize: [28, 36],

                iconAnchor: [12, 41],

                popupAnchor: [1, -34]

            });

            var mark = L.marker(bounds.getCenter(), {

                icon: customIcon

            }).addTo(map);



            var popup = L.popup({

                    closeOnClick: false,

                    autoClose: false,

                })

                .setLatLng(bounds.getCenter()) // Tentukan lokasi popup

                .setContent(data.jobsite); // Tetapkan konten popup



            // Buka popup secara otomatis

            popup.openOn(map);

            popups.push(popup)

            layers.push(mark);

            mark.bindPopup(popup);

            mark.on("click", function() {

                layers.forEach(layer => {

                    map.removeLayer(layer);

                });

                generateMarkerLocation(data);

                generateMarkerInfo(data.markerInfo)

                $(".marker-info").show()

                map.removeLayer(mark);

                const markerCoordinates = data.markers.map(marker => [marker.latitude, marker.longitude])

                const bounds = L.latLngBounds(markerCoordinates);

                map.fitBounds(bounds);

                mark.openPopup();

            })

        }



        function generateMarkerLocation(data) {

            data.markers.forEach(marker => {

                const label = marker['parent_new_code'].label.replaceAll(' ', '').toLowerCase();

                const color = markerRingColor[marker.color || "#36AE7C"];

                const iconUrl = `https://demo.sosioapps.co.id/markers/img/marker-${label}.png`;

                var customIcon = L.icon({

                    iconUrl: iconUrl,

                    iconSize: [28, 36],

                    iconAnchor: [12, 41],

                    popupAnchor: [1, -34]

                });



                var mark = L.marker([marker.latitude, marker.longitude], {

                    icon: customIcon

                });

                var popup = L.popup({

                        closeOnClick: false,

                        autoClose: false,

                    })

                    .setLatLng([marker.latitude, marker.longitude]) // Tentukan lokasi popup

                    .setContent(marker.location); // Tetapkan konten popup



                // Buka popup secara otomatis

                mark.bindPopup(popup);

                popup.openOn(map);

                mark.on("mouseover", function(e) {

                    this.openPopup();

                });



                popups.push(popup)

                layers.push(mark);

                map.addLayer(mark)



                mark.on("click", function() {

                    showData(marker.stakeholder || [], "stakeholder", "stakeholder")

                    showData(marker.communications || [], "isu", "communication", marker.location)

                    mark.openPopup();

                    map.setView([marker.latitude, marker.longitude]);

                    // Mengatur CSS untuk semua popups

                    $(".leaflet-popup-content-wrapper, .leaflet-popup-tip").css({

                        "background": "white",

                        "color": "black"

                    });



                    // Mengatur CSS untuk popup spesifik pada marker yang diklik

                    $(mark.getPopup().getElement()).find(

                        ".leaflet-popup-content-wrapper, .leaflet-popup-tip").css({

                        "background": "#EB5353",

                        "color": "white"

                    });

                })

            });



        }



        function setHeatmap (coordinates) {

            let heatMapLayer = coordinates.map(item => {

                let lat = parseFloat(item[0]);

                let lng = parseFloat(item[1]);

                let intensity = item[2]; // Normalize intensity (scale between 0.1 and 1.0)

                intensity = parseFloat(intensity.toFixed(2)); // Round to 1 decimal place



                return [lat, lng, intensity];

            })

            var options = {

                radius: 30,

                blur: 2,

                maxZoom: 10,

                gradient: {

                    0.25: '#36AE7C',

                    0.5: '#F4C542',

                    0.75: '#F57C00',

                    1: '#EB5353'

                }

            }

            var heat = L.heatLayer(heatMapLayer, options).addTo(map);

        }



        generateMarker();



        $('#change-jobsite-form').on('submit', function (e) {

            $('#jobsite').modal('hide')

        })

        $('#change-period-form').on('submit', function (e) {

            $('#periode').modal('hide')

        })

    </script>
